Theoretically the energy emitted from a transmitter, other things being 




voltage. 

The ultra-sonic waves are generated by the piezo-electric displacements in 
the quartz plate of the transmitter. The amplitude of the ultra-sonic wave is 
therefore proportional to the piezo-electric displacement in the quartz, which 


is proportional to the voltage applied to the instrument. Since the 



Three series of experiments were taken. Series 1. was taken at a frequency 
of 45,000 cycles per second; series £. at a frequency of 75,000 cycles, and series 
3. at 135,000 oycles, the last being the resomant frequency of the transmitter. 















In all cases the distance from the Transmitter wae 73 centimetres
